        		<script>var TrackingQueryString = function () {
	// This function is anonymous, is executed immediately and
	// the return value is assigned to QueryString!
	var query_string = {};
	var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
	var vars = query.split("&");
	for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
		var pair = vars[i].split("=");
			// If first entry with this name
		if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
		query_string[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1]);
			// If second entry with this name
		} else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
		var arr = [ query_string[pair[0]],decodeURIComponent(pair[1]) ];
		query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
			// If third or later entry with this name
		} else {
		query_string[pair[0]].push(decodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
		}
	}
	return query_string;
    }();

	function generateGUID() {
		let m='xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx', i= 0, u= '';
		while(i++<36) {
			let c = m[i-1],r= Math.random()*16|0, v= c=='x' ? r : (r&0x3|0x8);
			u += (c=='-'||c=='4') ? c : v.toString(16);
		}
		return u.toUpperCase();
	}

	if (typeof userGUID === 'undefined') {
		var userGUID = generateGUID();
	}

    </script>

    <div id="qr-faq">
    	
        <div class="qr-container">
            <h2 class="qr-faq-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
            <div class="qr-faq-items"><h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is a QR code? </h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">QR code is short for Quick Response code. QR codes are barcodes made up of colored squares on a contrasting background, which can be scanned using the camera on your mobile phone. <strong>The data encrypted in QR codes normally directs you to a website, app, phone number, or email address</strong>. They save time, and reduce the risk of error, by eliminating the need to manually enter a URL. They are commonly used in restaurants for non-contact menus, as trackable promotions for retail companies, and you will often see them in newspapers, on billboards, and even on clothing.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is a QR code generator? </h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">A QR code generator is a tool to help you quickly and easily create a custom QR code. <strong>Once you have finished generating your QR code you can download it and embed it in your website, landing page, or email newsletter, or you can print and display it</strong>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Will my QR code expire?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">As long as the data you are encrypting doesn&#8217;t expire, then the QR code will not expire. If, for example, you encrypt a URL that, at some point, no longer exists, those who scan the QR code will be redirected to a 404 page.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Are QR codes free? </h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes, our tool generates QR codes for free. There are no limitations on the number of QR codes you can create using our tool.</span> 
</div>
